4D metric tensor:
${{{ g} _u} _v} = {\overset{u\downarrow v\rightarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {g_{11}} & {g_{12}} & {g_{13}} & {g_{14}} \\ {g_{21}} & {g_{22}} & {g_{23}} & {g_{24}} \\ {g_{31}} & {g_{32}} & {g_{33}} & {g_{34}} \\ {g_{41}} & {g_{42}} & {g_{43}} & {g_{44}}\end{matrix} \right]}}$
4D metric tensor inverse
${{{ g} ^u} ^v} = {\overset{u\downarrow v\rightarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {g^{11}} & {g^{12}} & {g^{13}} & {g^{14}} \\ {g^{21}} & {g^{22}} & {g^{23}} & {g^{24}} \\ {g^{31}} & {g^{32}} & {g^{33}} & {g^{34}} \\ {g^{41}} & {g^{42}} & {g^{43}} & {g^{44}}\end{matrix} \right]}}$
EM potential vector:
${{ A} _u} = {\overset{u\downarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {A_1} \\ {A_2} \\ {A_3} \\ {A_4}\end{matrix} \right]}}$
${{ A} ^u} = {\overset{u\downarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {A^1} \\ {A^2} \\ {A^3} \\ {A^4}\end{matrix} \right]}}$
${{A^2}} = {{{{{A^1}}} \cdot {{{A_1}}}} + {{{{A^2}}} \cdot {{{A_2}}}} + {{{{A^3}}} \cdot {{{A_3}}}} + {{{{A^4}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}}}}$
5D metric tensor:
${{{ \tilde{g}} _a} _b} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {{g_{11}}} + {{{{{A_1}}^{2}}} {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{12}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{13}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{14}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} \\ {{g_{21}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{22}}} + {{{{{A_2}}^{2}}} {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{23}}} + {{{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{24}}} + {{{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} \\ {{g_{31}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{32}}} + {{{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{33}}} + {{{{{A_3}}^{2}}} {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{34}}} + {{{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} \\ {{g_{41}}} + {{{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{42}}} + {{{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{43}}} + {{{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{g_{44}}} + {{{{{A_4}}^{2}}} {{{\phi}^{2}}}} & {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} \\ {{{A_1}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} & {{{A_2}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} & {{{A_3}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} & {{{A_4}}} \cdot {{{\phi}^{2}}} & {\phi}^{2}\end{matrix} \right]}}$
5D metric tensor inverse:
${{{ \tilde{g}} ^a} ^b} = {{{ \overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[ \begin{matrix} {g^{11}} & {g^{12}} & {g^{13}} & {g^{14}} & -{{A^1}} \\ {g^{21}} & {g^{22}} & {g^{23}} & {g^{24}} & -{{A^2}} \\ {g^{31}} & {g^{32}} & {g^{33}} & {g^{34}} & -{{A^3}} \\ {g^{41}} & {g^{42}} & {g^{43}} & {g^{44}} & -{{A^4}} \\ -{{A^1}} & -{{A^2}} & -{{A^3}} & -{{A^4}} & {{A^2}} + {{\phi}^{-2}}\end{matrix} \right]}} ^a} ^b}$
